# pm-substrate Research Ledger

Last updated: 2026-07-13
Purpose: single shared ledger for research produced by humans, Codex runs, and scheduled automations.

This file is the cross-stream research current-state view. Chain-specific indexes still own detailed version history, but this ledger records the main claims, status changes, and implementation implications across all research streams.

## Run Protocol

Every research automation or manual research run must:

1. `git fetch origin main`.
2. Fast-forward or pull `main` before writing new research.
3. Inspect changed files from upstream, especially `research/`, `Changelog.md`, `packages/agent-state`, `packages/evals`, `packages/capability-finance-research-ingest`, `packages/continuity`, workflow, registry, graph, and event packages.
4. Read this ledger and the relevant chain-specific index.
5. Create a new versioned research file; never overwrite old versions.
6. Update the chain-specific index.
7. Update this ledger with new claims, corrected claims, downgraded claims, and implementation implications.
8. Update `Changelog.md` for material repo artifacts.
9. Run validation appropriate to the change.
10. Commit and push to `main`.

This protocol is itself an agent-state test: multiple actors are writing observations into one repo, and the repo must preserve provenance, reconcile parallel work, and expose current research state.

## Current Implementation Frontier

Current SQ frontier (2026-06-27 v228): `@pm/agent-state` now includes authority epoch seal accountable finality evidence. `buildOperationalStateAuthorityEpochSealAccountableFinalityEvidence()` creates a deterministic evidence envelope from two admitted finalizer-proof records; `evaluateOperationalStateAuthorityEpochSealAccountableFinalityEvidence()` recomputes finalizer proof hashes, admission record hashes, certificate hashes, shared accepted witnesses, conflict kinds, conflict hash, and evidence hash; and `evaluateOperationalStateAuthorityEpochSealFinalizer({ accountableFinalityEvidence })` can reject an otherwise valid finalizer proof when replayable evidence proves a conflicting admitted finalizer quorum for the same sealed subject frontier. Migration `0145` starts append-only evidence storage with subject identity, finalizer proof hashes, admission record hashes, certificate hashes, shared witnesses, conflict kinds, conflict hash, evidence body, and evidence hash. This closes known-conflict finality obstruction. It does not close finality-evidence gossip/custody/currentness, bootstrap-settlement split-history transparency, bootstrap-settlement record authority, privacy-proof verifier authority, SoD verifier authority, compaction-checkpoint admission witness/currentness, quorum-subsumption for heterogeneous authority systems, semantics-migration/state-transformer admission, settlement-authority admission/currentness, transparency-head currentness/gossip, or live Postgres privilege/restart proof. The next substrate boundary is SQ176 bootstrap-settlement transparency, followed by SQ177 bootstrap-settlement record authority, SQ178 privacy-proof verifier-authority admission, SQ179 SoD verifier-authority admission, SQ180 compaction-checkpoint witness/currentness, SQ181 quorum-subsumption beyond pairwise intersection, SQ182 semantics migration, SQ183 settlement-authority admission/currentness, SQ184 transparency-head currentness, and SQ185 finality-evidence gossip/custody/currentness.

Current SQ frontier (2026-06-27 v226): `@pm/agent-state` now includes authority-topology settlement proofs. `buildOperationalStateAuthorityTopologySettlementCandidate()` creates hash-bound competing topology branch candidates; `buildOperationalStateAuthorityTopologySettlementProof()` binds a candidate set, selected branch, recovery subject, settled topology hash, settlement authority boundary, and settlement certificate; `evaluateOperationalStateAuthorityTopologySettlementProof()` recomputes candidate hashes, candidate-set hash, settlement-claim hash, certificate binding, quorum sufficiency, and selected topology equality; and `evaluateOperationalStateAuthorityTopologyCompaction({ requireTopologySettlementProof: true })` can reject compacted authority recovery when branch settlement is missing, mismatched, false, or certified by the wrong authority boundary. Migration `0143` starts append-only proof storage with subject, candidate-set, selected-branch, certificate, and proof fields. This closes the first topology branch-settlement primitive. It does not close settlement-authority admission/currentness, verifier-role metadata/key-transparency settlement, accountable finality evidence, bootstrap-settlement split-history transparency, bootstrap-settlement record authority, privacy-proof verifier authority, SoD verifier authority, compaction-checkpoint admission witness/currentness, quorum-subsumption for heterogeneous authority systems, semantics-migration/state-transformer admission, or live Postgres privilege/restart proof. The next substrate boundary is SQ174 verifier-role metadata/key-transparency settlement, followed by SQ175 accountable finality evidence, SQ176 bootstrap-settlement transparency, SQ177 bootstrap-settlement record authority, SQ178 privacy-proof verifier-authority admission, SQ179 SoD verifier-authority admission, SQ180 compaction-checkpoint witness/currentness, SQ181 quorum-subsumption beyond pairwise intersection, SQ182 semantics migration, and SQ183 settlement-authority admission/currentness.

Current SQ frontier (2026-06-27 v227): `@pm/agent-state` now includes signature-verifier role settlement proofs. `buildOperationalStateSignatureVerifierRoleSettlementProof()` creates a hash-bound proof over verifier role metadata and transparency evidence; `evaluateOperationalStateSignatureVerifierRoleSettlementProof()` recomputes role metadata hash, settlement claim hash, proof hash, certificate binding, quorum sufficiency, allowed-claim boundaries, validity frontier, and transparency evidence presence; and `evaluateOperationalStateSignatureVerifierAdapterProof({ requireVerifierRoleSettlementProof: true })` can reject verifier adapter proofs when verifier role authority is missing, local-only, stale, overbroad, or certified by the wrong settlement boundary. Migration `0144` starts append-only proof storage with verifier role metadata, transparency-log, settlement-certificate, and proof fields. This closes the first verifier-role metadata/key-transparency settlement primitive. It does not close transparency-head currentness/gossip, settlement-authority admission/currentness, accountable finality evidence, bootstrap-settlement split-history transparency, bootstrap-settlement record authority, privacy-proof verifier authority, SoD verifier authority, compaction-checkpoint admission witness/currentness, quorum-subsumption for heterogeneous authority systems, semantics-migration/state-transformer admission, or live Postgres privilege/restart proof. The next substrate boundary is SQ175 accountable finality evidence, followed by SQ176 bootstrap-settlement transparency, SQ177 bootstrap-settlement record authority, SQ178 privacy-proof verifier-authority admission, SQ179 SoD verifier-authority admission, SQ180 compaction-checkpoint witness/currentness, SQ181 quorum-subsumption beyond pairwise intersection, SQ182 semantics migration, SQ183 settlement-authority admission/currentness, and SQ184 transparency-head currentness.

Current SQ frontier (2026-06-27 v225): `@pm/agent-state` now includes authority-transition replay-semantics proofs. `buildCurrentOperationalStateAuthorityTransitionReplaySemanticsManifest()` creates a hash-bound manifest for the authority transition algebra; `buildOperationalStateAuthorityTransitionReplaySemanticsProof()` binds retained transition records to manifest rule hashes and recovered topology output; `evaluateOperationalStateAuthorityTransitionReplaySemanticsProof()` recomputes the manifest, manifest validity frontier, rule hashes, transition bindings, sequence/hash-chain continuity, and result topology; and `evaluateOperationalStateAuthorityTopologyCompaction({ requireReplaySemanticsProof: true })` can reject compacted authority recovery when replay semantics are missing, stale, out of range, mismatched, or false. Migration `0142` starts append-only proof storage with subject, manifest, transition-binding, and result-topology fields. This closes the first replay-semantics versioning proof primitive. Current SQ frontier (2026-06-27 v165): `@pm/agent-state` can now recover nested pruning/currentness layers from admitted transition history through generic recovery cuts, recovery-cut admission records, recovery-cut admission witness records, signed history-root transparency observations, history-root settlement records, admitted pruning-policy artifacts, pruning-policy admission witness records, storage mutation guard authorization admission records, storage mutation guard authorization admission witness records, tombstone-history checkpoint admission witness records, witness-ledger checkpoint admission witness records, tombstone-history compaction checkpoint admission records, witness-ledger compaction checkpoint admission records, quorum-certificate proof-record admission records, quorum-certificate proof-record admission witness records, authority-topology compaction checkpoint admission records, signature-verifier proof admission records, authority epoch seal finalizer-proof admission records, compiled pruning-policy obligations, storage mutation guards, compacted tombstone-history replay, compacted witness-ledger replay, quorum-certificate proof-record replay, compacted authority-topology replay, constrained signature-verifier adapter proof replay, and authority epoch seal finalizer proof replay. `OperationalStateRecoveryCut` inventories replayable lanes and refuses private/cached required state; `OperationalStateRecoveryCutAdmissionRecord` makes the cut itself replay from durable, hash-linked admission history bound to the current-state view identity; `OperationalStateRecoveryCutAdmissionWitnessRecord` makes that latest admission row accountable through a separate quorum-certified witness ledger over the exact admission record hash; `OperationalStateHistoryRootObserverSignatureProof` makes strict root transparency accept only replay-current signed observer statements before roots bless recovery or create split-history obstructions; `OperationalStateHistoryRootSettlementRecord` makes strict recovery-root currentness replay from quorum-certified settlement history over exact root commitments before witnessed roots can bless recovery; `OperationalStatePruningPolicyCompilation` derives the canonical pruning/recovery ladder into lane obligations; `OperationalStatePruningPolicyAdmissionRecord` makes that compiled policy replay as the latest durable policy artifact before its obligations can authorize action; `OperationalStatePruningPolicyAdmissionWitnessRecord` makes that latest policy-admission row accountable through a separate quorum-certified witness ledger over the exact policy record hash; `OperationalStateStorageMutationGuardAuthorizationAdmissionRecord` makes physical storage mutation authorization rows replay as latest procedure/role-scoped admitted transitions before protected UPDATE/DELETE can proceed; `OperationalStateStorageMutationGuardAuthorizationAdmissionWitnessRecord` makes that latest guard-admission row accountable through a separate quorum-certified witness ledger over the exact guard/table/operation admission record hash; `OperationalStateTombstoneHistoryCompactionCheckpointAdmissionRecord` makes compacted tombstone-history checkpoint seeds replay as latest quorum-certified admitted transitions before strict compacted recovery can consume them; `OperationalStateTombstoneHistoryCompactionCheckpointAdmissionWitnessRecord` makes that latest tombstone checkpoint-admission row accountable through a separate quorum-certified witness ledger over the exact checkpoint-admission record hash; `OperationalStateWitnessLedgerCompactionCheckpointAdmissionRecord` makes compacted witness-ledger checkpoint seeds replay as latest quorum-certified admitted transitions before strict compacted witness recovery can consume them; `OperationalStateWitnessLedgerCompactionCheckpointAdmissionWitnessRecord` makes that latest witness-ledger checkpoint-admission row accountable through a separate quorum-certified witness ledger over the exact checkpoint-admission record hash; `OperationalStateQuorumCertificateProofRecordAdmissionRecord` makes generic quorum-certificate proof records replay as latest quorum-certified admitted transitions before strict recovered certified currentness can consume them; `OperationalStateQuorumCertificateProofRecordAdmissionWitnessRecord` makes that latest proof-record admission row accountable through a separate quorum-certified witness ledger over the exact admission record hash; `OperationalStateAuthorityTopologyCompactionCheckpointAdmissionRecord` makes compacted authority-topology checkpoint seeds replay as latest quorum-certified admitted transitions before strict compacted topology recovery can consume them; `OperationalStateSignatureVerifierAdapterProofAdmissionRecord` makes constrained verifier proofs replay as latest quorum-certified admitted transitions for their verification id before strict signature state can consume them; `OperationalStateAuthorityEpochSealFinalizerProofAdmissionRecord` makes authority epoch seal finalizer proofs replay as latest quorum-certified admitted transitions for their seal id before strict seal finality can consume them; `OperationalStateStorageMutationGuard` compiles protected-table DELETE/UPDATE guards that require tombstone-derived authorization and can now require latest witnessed guard-admission history; `OperationalStateTombstoneHistoryCompaction` proves compacted tombstone histories only when a checkpoint seed plus retained suffix reaches the exact required head; `OperationalStateWitnessLedgerCompaction` proves compacted witness histories only when a checkpoint seed plus retained suffix reconstructs the exact required accepted head and can now require latest witnessed checkpoint-admission history; `OperationalStateQuorumCertificateProofRecord` proves certified currentness only when admitted proof records reconstruct the exact required certificate with accepted evidence and seal linkage and can now require latest witnessed proof-record admission history; `OperationalStateAuthorityTopologyCompaction` proves compacted authority topology only when a checkpoint seed plus retained authority-transition suffix reconstructs the exact required topology; `OperationalStateSignatureVerifierAdapterProof` proves cryptographic signature validity only when bound to replayed key material, free of adapter-side authority/currentness claims, and admitted when strict proof admission is required; and `OperationalStateAuthorityEpochSealFinalizerProof` proves seal finality only when a replay-current finalizer signs the exact canonical seal payload through that constrained verifier boundary and the proof is admitted when strict finalizer-proof admission is required. This closes tombstone-history checkpoint admission, witness-ledger checkpoint admission, generic proof-record authority admission, authority-topology checkpoint admission, verifier-proof admission, Status note (2026-06-25): the previous 20-item frontier was implemented as pure tested primitives on 2026-06-10 in `@pm/agent-state` (`external-evidence.ts`), `@pm/evals` (`evidence-admission.ts`), and `@pm/capability-finance-research-ingest` (clean-current fixture). June 11 work committed replay corpora for evidence admission, ArrowHedge state-review artifacts, and write-binding attempts. tenant-aligned cross-corpus fixtures. v13 partially closed the v12 memory frontier as a pure/replay primitive. v14 partially closed the v12 receipt frontier as a pure/replay primitive: `target_receipt` is a first-class evidence kind, dispatch-only pseudo-receipts warn instead of reading as delivery proof, and replay metrics distinguish dispatch-only from applied receipts. v15 is v65 addendum: SQ12 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has `ProjectionReplayCertificateRef`, durable certificate record/store semantics, in-memory and Postgres certificate stores, and hash-bound projection-name admission for write-authority-grade certificates. Migration `0024_agent_state_projection_replay_certificates.sql` adds `agent_state.projection_replay_certificates`; `ActionOutcomeEnvelope` and eval packet recovery preserve `projectionReplayRef`; `@pm/capability-kit` can verify replay refs against a certificate store before returning write authority to capability `apply()`. The next proof is SQ13: add a tamper-evident certificate-store root and membership/consistency proof.

v66 addendum: SQ13 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has append-only projection replay certificate-store entries/roots, root-bound replay refs, chain consistency proof verification, and strict store-commitment verification. Migration `0025_agent_state_projection_replay_certificate_store_root.sql` adds the certificate-store entry ledger; `@pm/graph` preserves root fields structurally; `@pm/capability-kit` can require `requireProjectionReplayStoreCommitment` before returning authority. The next proof is SQ14: add root witnessing/gossip so divergent roots become obstructions across agents and resumes.

v67 addendum: SQ14 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has root witness admission, an in-memory witness, and obstruction artifacts for forked/regressed/tenant-mismatched/unproved/invalidly proved roots. `@pm/capability-kit` can pass root observations and consistency proofs to a structural witness before workflow-derived graph authority is returned. The next proof is SQ15: persist or quorum-prove root-witness observations so the witness layer itself is replayable.

v68 addendum: SQ15 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has hash-linked root-witness observation records, deterministic witness record hashing, ledger replay with decision recomputation, in-memory and Postgres witness ledgers, and a ledger-backed witness that recovers accepted roots after restart. Migration `0026_agent_state_projection_replay_root_witness.sql` adds the durable witness observation table. The next proof is SQ16: define quorum/finality semantics over witness ledgers.

v69 addendum: SQ16 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has root-witness settlement semantics over replayed witness ledgers: explicit required/minimum witness thresholds, `provisional` / `witnessed` / `settled` / `obstructed` status, invalid-ledger and duplicate-witness refusal, same-sequence conflicting-root obstruction, and deterministic settlement hashing. The next proof is SQ17: register settlement-eligible witness principals with replayable membership epochs, revocation, and equivocation handling.

v70 addendum: SQ17 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has hash-linked witness-authority transitions, deterministic authority transition hashing, topology replay at a certificate-store root sequence, active witness-principal projection, and settlement gating through replayed eligibility. Topology-bound settlement refuses non-member and equivocated witness ledgers and obstructs invalid topology replay. The next proof is SQ18: persist authority transitions and settlement certificates in substrate-owned durable stores.

v71 addendum: SQ18 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has durable witness-authority transition stores, durable settlement-record stores, settlement-record replay, and migration `0027_agent_state_projection_replay_witness_authority_settlement.sql`. Tampered authority transitions invalidate topology replay, and tampered settlement records cannot replay as settled roots. The next proof is SQ19: require durable settled-root certificates in strict graph/capability write gates before mutation.

v72 addendum: SQ19 is closed. `@pm/graph` now has `GraphWriteProjectionReplayRootSettlementRef` and `requireProjectionReplayRootSettlementRef`; `@pm/capability-kit` can verify settled-root refs against a durable settlement store before constructing graph authority; `@pm/agent-state` can build and verify settlement refs; and eval packet recovery preserves the proof. The next proof is SQ20: settlement-currentness/status so stale historical settlement refs cannot authorize later writes.

v73 addendum: SQ20 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has `ProjectionReplayCertificateStoreRootWitnessSettlementCurrentnessPolicy`, stale/conflict/frontier/topology issue codes, and settlement-store currentness verification; `@pm/capability-kit` passes currentness policy to the settlement store before constructing graph authority. The next proof is SQ21: settlement-store head transparency or witnessing so hidden truncation/forked settlement history cannot satisfy currentness policy.

v74 addendum: SQ21 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has settlement-store heads, required-head currentness verification, head consistency proofs, replayable head-witness records, in-memory and ledger-backed settlement-head witnesses, and `@pm/capability-kit` can witness a settlement-store head before settled-root verification. The next proof is SQ22: durable cross-agent settlement-head witness storage or gossip.

v75 addendum: SQ22 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has `PostgresProjectionReplayCertificateStoreRootWitnessSettlementStoreHeadWitnessLedger`, migration `0028_agent_state_projection_replay_settlement_head_witness.sql`, and a cross-agent shared-ledger regression test proving a fresh ledger-backed agent rejects an old head after another agent witnessed a newer head. The next proof is SQ23: settlement-head witness quorum/topology.

v76 addendum: SQ23 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has settlement-sequence-scoped head-witness authority transitions, replayed eligible principals, and head-witness quorum certificates; `@pm/capability-kit` can require a certified head quorum before returning graph write authority. The next proof is SQ24: durable head-witness authority-transition or quorum-certificate storage so adapters cannot supply synthetic topology.

v77 addendum: SQ24 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now has durable settlement-head witness authority-transition stores, migration `0029_agent_state_projection_replay_settlement_head_witness_authority.sql`, and a store-backed quorum certifier that replays topology from stored transitions plus head-witness records before certification. The next proof is SQ25: non-retroactive authority epochs or durable quorum-certificate finality so later topology transitions cannot rewrite prior head-certification authority.

v78 addendum: SQ25 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models `seal_authority_epoch` as a replayed settlement-head witness authority transition, exposes `effectiveAuthorityHash` and `authorityEpochSeals`, rejects retroactive topology appends after a sealed epoch, and obstructs tampered post-seal retroactive history during store-backed certification. The next proof is SQ26: signature-bearing witness and finalizer identity for observations, quorum certificates, and authority-epoch seals.

v79 addendum: SQ26 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models signature-bound settlement-head witness identity, including signed observation payloads, signed authority-epoch seals, admitted key metadata in replayed principal state, strict signature-policy replay, durable signature columns via migration `0030`, and store-backed certification obstruction for unsigned or wrong-key rows. The next proof is SQ27: durable quorum-certificate records binding witness signatures and epoch seals into recoverable proof objects.

v80 addendum: SQ27 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models durable settlement-head quorum-certificate proof records, including accepted witness evidence, observation hashes/signatures, optional epoch-seal linkage, record hashing, record-chain replay, in-memory/Postgres stores, migration `0031`, and tampered evidence/seal obstruction. The next proof is SQ28: key-status and rotation semantics for witness signatures.

v81 addendum: SQ28 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models settlement-head witness signature key status with replayed `rotate_signature_key` and `revoke_signature_key` transitions, principal key-status projection, strict current-key checks for witness records, authority-epoch seals, and quorum-certificate records, plus record-store append enforcement under strict policy. The next proof is SQ29: proof-preserving compaction for witness ledgers, key histories, and certificate records.

v82 addendum: SQ29 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models settlement-head witness replay compaction checkpoints, including witness-ledger, authority-topology, and quorum-certificate-record snapshots with compacted sequence/hash frontiers and checkpoint hashing. Replay can resume from checkpoint-plus-suffix and rejects suffixes without checkpoints or tampered checkpoint bodies. The next proof is SQ30: checkpoint-admission authority so arbitrary hash-valid snapshots cannot replace transition-derived state.

v83 addendum: SQ30 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models settlement-head witness replay compaction checkpoint admission certificates, including checkpoint-hash-bound witness evidence, strict signature-policy validation, current-key checks, quorum thresholds, admission hashing, and replay validation before any checkpoint can seed witness-ledger, authority/key-history, or quorum-certificate-record replay. The next proof is SQ31: durable checkpoint-admission storage and consistency proof.

v84 addendum: SQ31 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models durable settlement-head witness replay compaction checkpoint-admission records, including checkpoint/admission co-storage, record hashing, sequence and previous-hash replay, admission re-evaluation, checkpoint-id/frontier conflict detection, in-memory/Postgres stores, and migration `0032`. The next proof is SQ32: pruning admission rules for physical prefix deletion.

v85 addendum: SQ32 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models settlement-head witness replay compaction pruning admission, including durable checkpoint-admission record replay, suffix continuity validation for witness, authority, and quorum-certificate lanes, deterministic pruning-admission hashing, and focused falsification tests. The next proof is SQ33: tombstone-backed store pruning APIs.

v86 addendum: SQ33 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models settlement-head witness replay compaction pruning tombstones, including hash-linked tombstone replay, admitted pruning/checkpoint material binding, tombstone-gated physical prune methods for witness/authority/quorum stores, pruned-store continuity checks, and migration `0033`. The next proof is SQ34: tombstone-head witnessing and consistency proofs.

v87 addendum: SQ34 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models pruning tombstone-store head currentness, including tombstone-store head hashing, head derivation from tombstone records, required-head matching in pruned-store continuity, and falsification tests for stale, forked, unwitnessed, and tampered heads. The next proof is SQ35: durable tombstone-head witness ledgers.

v88 addendum: SQ35 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models durable pruning tombstone-head witness ledgers, including observation decisions, hash-linked witness records, consistency-proof validation over pruning tombstones, in-memory/Postgres ledgers, a ledger-backed witness, migration `0034`, and falsification tests for replay-derived required heads, unproved advances, forks, and tampered witness decisions. The next proof is SQ36: tombstone-head witness authority topology and quorum.

v89 addendum: SQ36 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models pruning tombstone-head witness authority topology and quorum certificates, including hash-linked authority-transition replay, eligible observer projection, quorum-threshold projection, and certificate evaluation over replayed tombstone-head witness records. Focused tests prove two authorized witnesses can certify a tombstone head while a topology admitting only one observer leaves the head witnessed but uncertified. The next proof is SQ37: durable tombstone-head witness authority-transition stores.

v90 addendum: SQ37 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models durable pruning tombstone-head witness authority-transition stores, including in-memory/Postgres append/list implementations, migration `0035`, store-backed tombstone-head quorum certification, and focused tests proving stored sequence/hash chaining plus incomplete-store non-certification. The next proof is SQ38: tombstone-head authority epoch seals.

v91 addendum: SQ38 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models pruning tombstone-head authority epoch seals, including `seal_authority_epoch` transitions, sealed topology/certificate fields, replayed `authorityEpochSeals`, `effectiveAuthorityHash` preservation for historical certification, append-time retroactive-transition refusal, migration `0036`, and focused tests proving seal finality plus tampered-history obstruction. The next proof is SQ39: signature-bound tombstone-head witness identity.

v92 addendum: SQ39 is closed. `@pm/agent-state` now models signature-bound pruning tombstone-head witness identity, including tombstone-head observation signatures, tombstone-head authority-transition signatures, strict replay against `pruningTombstoneHeadAuthorityTopology`, signature-key metadata projection into tombstone-head principal state, migration `0037`, and focused tests proving signed quorum/seal success plus unsigned and wrong-key obstruction. The next proof is SQ40: durable tombstone-head quorum-certificate records.

Remaining frontier:

1. Expand the selected write-binding gate beyond the ArrowHedge replay/runtime fixture path: every write-capable capability transport must provide state-review artifact ids/hashes, evidence-admission review ids, and a policy disposition that is recomputed or verified against durable substrate stores before broad mutation-governance claims.
2. Promote the new fixture-backed `EvidenceBindingReferenceCatalog` sources from committed ArrowHedge state-review, evidence-admission, and write-binding JSONL into durable DB-backed or substrate-store-backed verification sources.
3. Expand the new transport coverage metrics beyond the fixture inventory so every real write-capable path is classified as `required_verified`, `advisory_only`, or `missing_provider`.
4. Exercise the MCP admission lane against a live MCP server (the fixture lane is pure; revalidation semantics against real handles/annotations are untested).
5. Run the write-binding corpus against a real DB-backed ArrowHedge workflow when `PM_DATABASE_URL` is available and compare it with the static JSONL replay stream.
6. Capture HyperTool-style nested tool subcall read/write refs so executable wrappers cannot hide dependencies from read-set validation.
7. Extend the new memory write/read influence lane with poisoned/stale denial cases, patch/supersession lineage, compaction replay fidelity, and runtime consumption by write bindings.
8. Add skill/compiled-rule governance fixtures for owner, trigger, scope, version, source, and fault coverage.
9. Run PM dependency-structure agreement (`comparePmHandoffAgreement`) over real multi-agent ArrowHedge runs, not synthetic facets, and add risk-capture/rediscovery/time-to-valid-action metrics.
10. Add trajectory release-budget fixtures before making privacy/release claims.
11. Add explicit policy-transition fixtures so admitted evidence cannot bypass workflow state machines or approval/escalation policy.
12. Add LLM-judge state-defect recall and judge-routing miss metrics.
13. Classify invariants by enforceability: pre-write enforceable, compensation-enforceable, monitorable-only, or offline-audit.
14. Track the rewrite-thesis instruments as ledger claims: ArrowHedge T1-T8 pass status and the 12 behavior metrics (time-to-plugin, substrate edit count, mapping coverage, etc.) — the plug-in half of the thesis has no research stream.
15. Competitive falsification attempts against vendor technical/SDK docs (ServiceNow dev portal, Atlassian Forge/Rovo, Asana developers) instead of press-release surfaces; add a plug-in-comparator scan (embedded iPaaS, schema-mapping vendors) against the zero-substrate-edit criterion.
16. Add target-side delivery confirmation for scheduled/subagent/memory/PM handoff writes before those writes become admitted operational state.
17. Add PM protocol-burden and role-utility metrics before expanding handoff scaffolding or multi-agent orchestration.
18. Add terminal outcome partition tests before claiming live governance from block events or dashboard gate counts.
19. ~~Update front-door docs (`README.md`, `docs/roadmap.md`, `docs/validation.md`) to the rewrite thesis so research and automation anchor on the current objective.~~ **Done 2026-06-10** — all four front-door docs rewritten (incl. `docs/architecture.md`); wedding-era packages removed from the workspace; validation re-anchored to ArrowHedge T1–T8 + 12 metrics (see Changelog "Wedding-era retirement").

## Open Watchlist

1. Continue daily AI competitive-intelligence monitoring for fresh primary evidence that vendors expose portable original-observation/read-set/action-review artifacts.
2. Inspect whether OpenAI, Anthropic, Microsoft, Google, AWS, ServiceNow, Atlassian, Asana, Cursor, Slack/Salesforce, or other major vendors are solving currentness, authority, provenance, workflow validity, and pre-action review, or only memory/RAG/context/session/workflow/audit.
3. Expand opt-in write binding across every external write transport and require durable catalog verification before claiming broad mutation enforcement.
4. Adopt storage mutation guard triggers and tombstone-derived authorization insertion in every Postgres pruning path, adopt tombstone-history/witness-ledger/authority-topology compaction checkpoints, quorum-certificate proof records, signature-verifier adapter proofs, authority epoch seal finalizer proofs, recovery-cut admission records, and history-root observer signature proofs in runtime stores, add role-separated/stored-procedure control for guard authorization rows, and add durable policy/recovery-cut admission authority so direct SQL DELETE/UPDATE, fake guard rows, stale compiled policies, verifier callbacks, unsigned finality rows, fake recovery cuts, unsigned root gossip, or compacted summaries cannot bypass tombstone-gated recovery authority.
5. Add trajectory release-budget, policy-transition conformance, and LLM-judge state-defect recall fixtures.
6. Treat future merge conflicts, fetch failures, Git object warnings, or stale local research as evidence for the substrate thesis and record how they were reconciled.
7. Watch whether GitHub exposes machine-readable third-party-agent validation artifacts that can be admitted as external evidence.
8. Watch whether model providers expose retention/admin-policy metadata through APIs or action artifacts.
9. Re-check MCP release status and SEP-2567 adoption in the dated spec before treating handle semantics as current protocol behavior.
10. Watch whether Copilot CLI `/security-review` emits machine-readable artifacts or status refs.
11. Watch whether Google Drive approvals expose revision/hash/scope metadata sufficient for approval-currentness validation.
12. Watch whether AWS AgentCore trace/eval/memory/identity schemas can map into an external evidence admission contract.
13. Watch whether Cursor custom stores and nested subagents expose provenance/freshness metadata.
14. Watch whether skill libraries expose version, trigger precision, scope, and fault-coverage metadata sufficient for substrate admission.
15. Watch whether executable tool wrappers expose nested subcall read/write refs or hide dependency edges behind a single outer call.
16. Watch whether memory-evolution and compaction systems expose source refs, supersession, deletion residue, and replayable patch histories.
17. Watch whether PM-oriented agent systems expose risk capture, source/owner agreement, escalation authority, and status-update cost as machine-readable evidence.
18. Watch whether agent infrastructure admits certificate/revocation/status artifacts before production mutation, not only audit logs after mutation.
19. Watch for target-side delivery confirmation in multi-agent orchestration and memory systems.
20. Watch for evidence that PM/human-AI scaffolding improves risk capture without increasing rework, quality loss, or diversity collapse.
